FNV PBR PPLIGHTING PASS-ENTRY ARG TABLE FOLLOW-UP AUDIT

Purpose:
1. Prove callsite argument order for E7F430, BA9EE0, BA8EC0, and BA8C50.
2. Capture ECX owners for thiscall helpers instead of relying on decompiler formatting.
3. Reduce PPLighting record and pass-entry helpers into mechanical argument tuples.

Interpretation rules:
- stack_arg0 is the first stack argument consumed by the callee, i.e. the last PUSH before CALL.
- E7F430 and BA9EE0 also use ECX as their owner/list object.
- BA9EE0 core layout already proved: arg0 -> entry +0, arg1 -> +4 word, arg2 -> +7 byte, arg3 -> +9 array count, arg4+ copied into entry +0xC array.
- Do not assign albedo/normal/roughness semantics until the argument rows are correlated with draw-time texture binding.
